<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rood.html>rood</a> (1397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">rôot</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">rōt</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*raudaz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁rowdʰós</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:root.html>root</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁rewdʰ-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective"><a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>Adjective</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rood.html>rood</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:roder.html>roder</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">roodst</b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:rotonde.html>rotonde</a> (30961)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotonde.html>rotonde</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">rotonda</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">rotondus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotonde.html>rotonde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotondes.html>rotondes</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">rotonden</b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:rotonde.html>rotondetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:roundabout.html>roundabout</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:road.html>road</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:junction.html>junction</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:at.html>at</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:traffic.html>traffic</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:streams.html>streams</a> circularly <a href = vnd.unilang:around.html>around</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:central.html>central</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:island.html>island</a>). <span class="defdate">[<a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ca.html>ca</a>. 1940]</span>
